  (define (set-x! v) (set! x v))
  (define (set-y! v) (set! y v))
  (define (dispatch m)

          ((eq? m 'cdr) y)
          ((eq? m 'set-car!) set-x!)
          ((eq? m 'set-cdr!) set-y!)
